## <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f357-1613">備註</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f357-1613">Remarks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f357-1614">**MS DFSR LocalSettings** 類別是 DFS 複寫服務支援的一部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f357-1614">The **ms-DFSR-LocalSettings** class is a part of the DFS Replication service support.</span></span>
